# War for Balkans
####
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.2
	title = ww1_ottoman.2.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		has_defensive_war_with = SER
		has_defensive_war_with = GRE
		has_defensive_war_with = BUL
		date < 1914.1.1
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = kis_war
		}	
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.2.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

###Civil war over, recovery idea
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.5
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_hareket_ordusu_uprising
			has_country_flag = TUR_nationalist_uprising
		}
		has_civil_war = no
		NOT = {
			has_idea = TUR_idea_recovery_civil_war
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_recovered_from_civil_war
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	immediate = {
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = TUR_idea_recovery_civil_war
			days = 360
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ww1_ottoman.6
			days = 360
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.6
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = TUR_recovered_from_civil_war
		remove_ideas = TUR_idea_recovery_civil_war
	}
}

	id = ww1_ottoman.7

		tag = TUR
		has_country_flag = TUR_recovered_from_civil_war
		has_civil_war = yes
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 0
	}
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = TUR_recovered_from_civil_war
	}
}

# Mehmed V death
####
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.8
	title = ww1_ottoman.8.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		date > 1918.7.2
		has_country_flag = yusuf_izzettin_suicide
		OR = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_mehmed_v
				ruling_only = no
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_osman_iv
				ruling_only = yes
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_abdulmecid_ii
				ruling_only = yes
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = interwar_mehmed_vi_succeeded_mehmed_v
			set_country_flag = TUR_mehmed_v_dies
			retire_character = TUR_mehmed_v
			TUR_mehmed_vi = {
				set_character_name = "TUR_mehmed_vi"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						character = TUR_mehmed_v
					}
				}
				promote_character = TUR_mehmed_vi
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
				}
				remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
				add_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_vi
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.8.a
	}
}

###Mehmed V dies Yusuf succeeds
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.9
	title = ww1_ottoman.9.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.9.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		date > 1918.7.2
		OR = {
			has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_mehmed_v
				ruling_only = no
			}
		}
		has_country_leader = {
			character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
			ruling_only = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = yusuf_izzettin_suicide
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_osman_iv
				ruling_only = yes
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_abdulmecid_ii
				ruling_only = yes
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.9.a
		set_country_flag = TUR_mehmed_v_dies
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascism
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		retire_character = TUR_mehmed_v
		TUR_yusuf_izzeddin = {
			set_character_name = "TUR_yusuf_i"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					character = TUR_mehmed_v
				}
			}
			promote_character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
			add_ideas = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
		}
	}
}

###Yusuf Izzettin dead
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.10
	title = ww1_ottoman.10.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.10.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_europe_funeral
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		date > 1916.2.1
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = mustafa_enver_cemal
			has_country_flag = TUR_three_pasha_government
			has_government = fascism
			has_global_flag = sevket_alive
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
			}
			has_idea = TUR_yusuf_izzettin
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.10.a
		retire_character = TUR_yusuf_izzeddin
		set_country_flag = yusuf_izzettin_suicide
		custom_effect_tooltip = vahdettin_succeeds_mehmed_tt
	}
}

	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		controls_state = 446
		controls_state = 447
		has_global_flag = kis_war
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.15.a
		set_country_flag = ottomans_hold_cairo_and_alexandria
	}
}

#We take Egypt after op- also by UU ;)
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.16
	title = ww1_ottoman.16.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_turkish_soldiers
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		has_country_flag = great_war_winner
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = ottomans_hold_cairo_and_alexandria
			has_subject = EGY
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = EGY
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.16.a
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = ENG
						is_owned_by = EGY
					}
					OR = {
						state = 447
						state = 453
					}
				}
				TUR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			ENG = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_subject = EGY
					}
					end_puppet = EGY
				}
			}
			EGY = {
				country_lock_all_division_template = no
				promote_character = EGY_abbas_ii_helmy			
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = ENG
						OR = {
							is_core_of = EGY
							is_core_of = SUD
							is_core_of = DAR
						}
					}
					EGY = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = LBA
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = EGY
						OR = {
							state = 552
							state = 767
						}
					}
					LBA = {
						transfer_state = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { EGY = { is_subject_of = TUR } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
				}
				TUR = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = EGY
						autonomous_state = autonomy_dominion
						freedom_level = 0.8
					}
				}
				else = {
					puppet = EGY
				}
				EGY = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_popularities = {
						democratic = 34
						neutrality = 65
					}
				}
			}
		}
		EGY = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TUR
				}
				transfer_state_to = TUR
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = EGY
						}
					}
				}
				TUR = {
					annex_country = {
						target = EGY
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		name = ww1_ottoman.17.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 55
		}
		give_guarantee = EGY

		}
	}
}

			factor = 95
		}
		add_state_claim = 447
		add_state_claim = 453
		create_wargoal = {
			type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			target = EGY
		}
		give_resource_rights = {
			receiver = GER
			state = 291
		}
		give_resource_rights = {
			receiver = GER
			state = 676
		}
		give_resource_rights = {
			receiver = GER
			state = 292
		}
		give_resource_rights = {
			receiver = GER
			state = 678
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_idea_german_blank_cheque

			set_global_flag = ottoman_egypt_guaranteed
		}
	}
	#on second thoughts...
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.18.b

			factor = 5
		}
	}

# Crisis: Hareket Ordusu (Third Army) against Islamists
####
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.22
	title = ww1_ottoman.22.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_sultan_in_istanbul
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = neutrality
				size = 0.35
				states = {
					356
					340
					339
					342
					164
					899
					790
					348
					354
					355
					353
					352
					758
					803
					106
					760
					761
					759
					788
					184
					731
					454
					756
					757
					858
					856
					852
				}
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
						has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
					}
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 18
					fascism = 64
					communism = 0
					neutrality = 18
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				keep_political_leader = yes
				PREV = {
       				TUR_ismail_enver = {
        			    set_nationality = PREV.PREV
        			}
    			}
				TUR_ismail_enver = {
					promote_character = despotism
					set_character_name = TUR_ismail_enver_pasha
					promote_leader = yes
					add_country_leader_trait = standing_alone
				}
				add_ideas = TUR_officers_struggle_harbiyeli_officers_org_1
				add_ideas = TUR_ittihadist_academy_spirit_no_remove
				set_variable = { var = opda_lira value = TUR.opda_lira }
				set_variable = { var = opda_consumer_goods value = TUR.opda_consumer_goods }
				set_variable = { var = opda_resources_to_market value = TUR.opda_resources_to_market }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_minorities }

				load_focus_tree = { tree = ottoman_focus_tree keep_completed = no }
				mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_aftermath_of_31_march_incident
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_glory_to_the_action_army
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_harbiyeli_officers
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_reaffirm_the_loyalty_of_the_army
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_elections_1912
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_undermine_democracy
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_three_pasha_government
				set_country_flag = TUR_revolter_flag
				set_cosmetic_tag = TUR_revolter
			}
			TUR = {
				TUR_ismail_enver = {
					set_nationality = OTT
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = TUR
					has_government = fascism
				}
				TUR_ismail_enver = {
					promote_character = despotism
					set_character_name = TUR_ismail_enver_pasha
					promote_leader = yes
					add_country_leader_trait = standing_alone
				}
				add_ideas = TUR_officers_struggle_harbiyeli_officers_org_1
				add_ideas = TUR_ittihadist_academy_spirit_no_remove
				set_variable = { var = opda_lira value = TUR.opda_lira }
				set_variable = { var = opda_consumer_goods value = TUR.opda_consumer_goods }
				set_variable = { var = opda_resources_to_market value = TUR.opda_resources_to_market }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_minorities }
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = standing_alone
			OTT = {
				TUR_ismail_enver = {
					promote_character = despotism
					set_character_name = TUR_ismail_enver_pasha
					promote_leader = yes
					add_country_leader_trait = standing_alone
				}
				add_ideas = TUR_officers_struggle_harbiyeli_officers_org_1
				add_ideas = TUR_ittihadist_academy_spirit_no_remove
				set_variable = { var = opda_lira value = TUR.opda_lira }
				set_variable = { var = opda_consumer_goods value = TUR.opda_consumer_goods }
				set_variable = { var = opda_resources_to_market value = TUR.opda_resources_to_market }
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_OPDA }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_hareket_ordusu_uprising
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.22.a
		news_event = ottoman.5
		set_country_flag = TUR_purge_radical_ittihadists
		set_country_flag = TUR_purge_ittihadists
		hidden_effect = {
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 5
				neutrality = 25
				fascism = 68
				communism = 2
			}
		}
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
					has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
				}
			}
			set_nationality = OTT
		}
		remove_ideas = TUR_ittihadist_academy_spirit_no_remove
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {

			uncomplete_national_focus = {
  				focus = TUR_elections_of_1912
  				uncomplete_children = yes
  				refund_political_power = no
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_savior_officer_coup
		add_ideas = TUR_government_without_majority
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		unlock_national_focus = TUR_savior_officer_coup
		remove_ideas = TUR_idea_liberal_revenge

			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = TUR_formulate_a_coup
					has_completed_focus = TUR_intervene_in_the_elections
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = ottoman.44
				hours = 89
			}
		}

			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_intervene_in_the_elections
			}

				id = ottoman.36

			}
		}

			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

# Crisis: Hareket Ordusu against Sultan
####
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.26
	title = ww1_ottoman.26.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.26.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_sultan_in_istanbul
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = fascism
				size = 0.25
				states = {
					356
					345
					355
					49
				}
				capital = 49
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
						has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
					}
				}
				keep_political_leader = yes			
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = ottoman_focus_tree
					keep_completed = no
				}

				unlock_national_focus = TUR_undermine_democracy
				unlock_national_focus = TUR_three_pasha_government
				set_country_flag = TUR_revolter_flag
				set_cosmetic_tag =  TUR_revolter
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = standing_alone
			TUR = {
				TUR_ismail_enver = {
					set_nationality = OTT
				}
			}
			OTT = {

						limit = {
							is_field_marshal = no									
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
					add_country_leader_trait = standing_alone
				}
			}	
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.26.a

		hidden_effect = {

				democratic = 5

# Crisis: Millet-i Osmaniye against Socialists
####
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.32
	title = ww1_ottoman.32.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.32.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_sultan_and_pashas
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = fascism
				size = 0.15
				states = {
					356
					345
					355
					49
				}
				capital = 49
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = ottoman_focus_tree
					keep_completed = no
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_legacy_of_31_march
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_choose_side
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_harbiyeli
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_reshape_the_army
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_hurriyet_musavat_uhuvvet
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_weaken_the_sultans_power
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_coup_of_savior_officers
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_raid_on_sublime_porte
					unlock_national_focus = TUR_empower_nazir_i_harbiye
				}
				add_ideas = TUR_sultan_mehmed_v
				set_country_flag = TUR_revolter_flag
				set_cosmetic_tag =  TUR_revolter
				keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
						has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
					}
				}
				keep_political_leader = yes
			}
			TUR = {
				TUR_ismail_enver = {
					set_nationality = OTT
				}
			}
			OTT = {	
				TUR_ismail_enver = {
					promote_character = fascism_ideology
					set_character_name = TUR_ismail_enver_pasha
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_field_marshal = no									
						}
						promote_leader = yes
					}
					add_country_leader_trait = standing_alone
				}
			}
			end_puppet = QAT
			QAT = {
				clr_country_flag = protectorate
			}
			end_puppet = KUW
			KUW = {
				clr_country_flag = protectorate
			}
			end_puppet = JBS
			add_country_leader_trait = standing_alone
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.32.a
		news_event = ottoman.5
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
					has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
				}
			}
			set_nationality = OTT
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_hareket_ordusu_uprising
		hidden_effect = {
			set_popularities = {
				democratic = 20
				communism = 50
				fascism = 10
				neutrality = 20
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_socialist_civilwar_elections
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

		QAT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				ROOT = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PREV
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
			give_military_access = ROOT
			ROOT = { give_guarantee = PREV }
			ENG = { give_guarantee = PREV }
			hidden_effect = {
				clr_country_flag = protectorate
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = PREV
					}
					white_peace = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		#reduce economy debuff
		#TUR_ODPA_level_up = yes
		news_event = ww1_ottoman.42
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.39.b		#Stop negotiations
		add_political_power = -15
		ENG = {
			country_event = {
				id = ww1_ottoman.41
				hours = 8
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# Franco-Syrian War
###############################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.45
	title = ww1_ottoman.45.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.45.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_soldiers_marching
	trigger = {
		tag = FRA
		has_country_flag = great_war_winner
		has_global_flag = versallies_treaty
		has_war = no
		is_neighbor_of = SYR
		SYR = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject = no
			has_war = no
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 80
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.45.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				IRQ = {
					exists = yes
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		SYR = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PREV
				modifier = medium_decrease
			}
		}
		#create_wargoal = {
		#	target = SYR
		#	type = annex_everything
		#}
		# i dont wanna harm interwar armistice
		annex_country = {
			target = SYR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.45.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				IRQ = {
					exists = no
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SYR
					is_claimed_by = SYR
					is_core_of = LEB
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 829
					state = 857
					state = 859
				}
			}
			SYR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 831
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = JBS
				}
				JBS = { transfer_state = 831 }
				else = {
					SYR = { transfer_state = 831 }
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = SYR
				is_claimed_by = FRA
			}
			remove_claim_by = FRA
		}
		SYR = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PREV
				modifier = medium_increase
			}
		}
	}
}

# Arabian Revolt - Deal with Faisal
######################################
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.46
	title = ww1_ottoman.46.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.46.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_sultan_and_pashas
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		any_state = {
			is_core_of = SYR
			NOT = {
				state = 680
				state = 829
			}
			is_owned_by = TUR
		}
		has_war_with = HJZ
		has_global_flag = great_arabian_revolt
		SYR = {
			exists = no
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = great_war_ends
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.46.a		#Independence for Syria
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = SYR
					is_claimed_by = SYR
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 680
					state = 829
					state = 857
					state = 859
				}
			}
			SYR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		puppet = SYR
		hidden_effect = {
			SYR = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
				}
				set_popularities = {
					neutrality = 100
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				has_war_with = HJZ
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				white_peace = HJZ
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				HJZ = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
						dismantle_faction = yes
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = {
							is_in_faction = yes
						}
						leave_faction = yes
					}
					white_peace = PREV
					set_truce = {
						target = PREV
						days = 365
					}
				}
			}
		}
		SYR = {
			give_military_access = HJZ
			give_guarantee = HJZ
		}
		HJZ = {
			give_military_access = SYR
			give_guarantee = SYR
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				surrender_progress < 0.05
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				HJZ = { has_capitulated = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.46.b		#Ignor Faisal
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TUR
				is_core_of = SYR
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						state = 829
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
					}
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = TUR
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}
}

###Darfur becomes free
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.70
	title = ww1_ottoman.70.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.70.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		trigger = {
			has_capitulated = no
		}
		#Based
		name = ww1_ottoman.70.a
		ENG = {
			end_puppet = DAR
			hidden_effect = {
				set_country_flag = darfur_free
			}
		}
		DAR = {
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = DAR
			}
			white_peace = DAR
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	option = {
		#We want still bri'ish protection
		name = ww1_ottoman.70.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

		}

		set_rule = {
			can_join_factions = yes
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
}

	id = ww1_ottoman.92
	title = ww1_ottoman.92.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.92.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_naval_treaty
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR		#will be decision
		GER = {
			exists = yes
		}
		date > 1910.9.12
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = GER
			has_global_flag = TUR_GER_battleship_purchase
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.92.a
		GER = {
			country_event = { id = ww1_ottoman.93 hours = 8 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.92.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}
}

# Sell Two Battleships To Ottoman

country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.93
	title = ww1_ottoman.93.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.93.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_naval_treaty
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.93.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = TUR_ottoman_ship_sale
			days = 90
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			transfer_ship = {
				prefer_name = "SMS Kurfürst Friedrich Wilhelm"
				type = battleship
				target = TUR
			}
			transfer_ship = {
				prefer_name = "SMS Weissenburg"
				type = battleship
				target = TUR
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			TUR = {
				country_event = { id = ww1_ottoman.94 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.93.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			TUR = {
				country_event = { id = ww1_ottoman.95 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
	}
}

# Sell ships
###########
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.94
	title = ww1_ottoman.94.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.94.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_naval_treaty
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.94.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_global_flag = TUR_GER_battleship_purchase
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = opda_lira
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_debt_0885
			add_to_variable = {
				opda_lira = 0.885
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				opda_consumer_goods = 0.03
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				opda_resources_to_market = 0.015
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_variable = opda_lira
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = TUR_german_ship_purchase
				days = 360
			}
		}
		GER = {
			transfer_ship = {
				prefer_name = "SMS Kurfürst Friedrich Wilhelm"
				type = battleship
				target = TUR
			}
			transfer_ship = {
				prefer_name = "SMS Weissenburg"
				type = battleship
				target = TUR
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.96
	title = ww1_ottoman.96.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.96.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_battle
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		has_war_with = GER
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = TUR
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.96.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		TUR = {
			country_event = ww1_ottoman.97
		}
		ENG = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
					}
				}
				load_oob = ENG_seized_naval_legacy
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Man the Guns"
				}
				load_oob = ENG_seized_naval_mtg
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.96.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		TUR = {
			country_event = ww1_ottoman.98
		}
	}
}

		JBS = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject_of = TUR
		}
		TUR = {
			owns_state = 292
			owns_state = 678
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.99.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		JBS = {
			transfer_state = 292
			add_state_core = 292
			transfer_state = 678
			add_state_core = 678
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.99.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		end_puppet = JBS
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = JBS
				has_war_with = TUR
			}
			white_peace = JBS
		}
		TUR = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = JBS
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}

# Indonesian Anti-Colonist Front
###########
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.101
	title = ww1_ottoman.101.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.101.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_fascist_gathering
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.101.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ruling_party = democratic
				ideology = neutrality
				size = 0.7
			}
			else = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.7
				}
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = INS
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = INS_OTT
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "TUR"
				value = 50
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "TUR"
				value = 200
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				division_template = {
					name = "Teskilat Brigade"
					regiments = {
						infantry = {
							x = 0
							y = 0
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 0
							y = 1
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 0
							y = 2
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 1
							y = 0
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 1
							y = 1
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 1
							y = 2
						}
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"1. Teskilat Brigade\" division_template = \"Teskilat Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
						owner = INS
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"2. Teskilat Brigade\" division_template = \"Teskilat Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = INS
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"3. Teskilat Brigade\" division_template = \"Teskilat Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = INS
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"4. Teskilat Brigade\" division_template = \"Teskilat Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = INS
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# Pakistan-Bangladesh Anti-Colonist Front
###########
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.102
	title = ww1_ottoman.102.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.102.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_fascist_gathering
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.102.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				PAK = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = PAK
				}
				PAK = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PAK
				type = annex_everything
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				PAK = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = neutrality
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = neutrality
				size = 0.7
				states = {
					430
					431
					432
					288
					435
				}
			}
			else = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.7
					states = {
						430
						431
						432
						288
						435
					}
				}
			}
		}
		PAK = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = PAK_OTT
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = befriend
				id = "TUR"
				value = 50
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = alliance
				id = "TUR"
				value = 200
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				division_template = {
					name = "Teskilat Brigade"

							x = 0
							y = 0
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 0
							y = 1
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 0
							y = 2
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 1
							y = 0
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 1
							y = 1
						}
						infantry = {
							x = 1
							y = 2
						}
					}
				}
				random_controlled_state = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"1. Teskilat Brigade\" division_template = \"Teskilat Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.4"
						owner = PREV
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"2. Teskilat Brigade\" division_template = \"Teskilat Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = PREV
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"3. Teskilat Brigade\" division_template = \"Teskilat Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = PREV
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"4. Teskilat Brigade\" division_template = \"Teskilat Brigade\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = PREV
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"1. Milis Kuvveti\" division_template = \"Milis Kuvveti\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = PREV
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"2. Milis Kuvveti\" division_template = \"Milis Kuvveti\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = PREV
					}
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"3. Milis Kuvveti\" division_template = \"Milis Kuvveti\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
						owner = PREV

		name = ottoman.3.a

			}

		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_sultanate_party
			long_name = TUR_sultanate_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date < 1914.1.10
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mehmed_said
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
   		        character = TUR_said_halim
    		    promote_leader = yes
    		    country_leader = {
        	    	ideology = theocracy_ideology
        	    	expire = "1965.1.1.1"
        	     	traits = { TUR_conservative_politician grand_vizier }
    		    }
		    }
		}
		TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.4.a
		every_unit_leader = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_sympathies
					has_trait = trait_TUR_ittihadist_radical_sympathies
				}
			}
			set_nationality = OTT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_government_without_majority
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_government_without_majority
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_ittihadist_plot
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_ittihadist_plot
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_sultanate_party
			long_name = TUR_sultanate_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date < 1914.1.10
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mehmed_said
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
   		        character = TUR_said_halim
    		    promote_leader = yes
    		    country_leader = {
        	    	ideology = theocracy_ideology
        	    	expire = "1965.1.1.1"
        	    	traits = { TUR_conservative_politician grand_vizier }
    		    }
		    }
		}
		TUR_remove_harbiyeli_officers = yes
		TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = ottoman.5 hours = 8 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

#Demand Annexation of Arabic Country
country_event = {
	id = ottoman.8
	title = ottoman.8.t
	desc = ottoman.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_turkish_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.8.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				annex_country = {
					target = ROOT
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = ottoman.9 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 50
				is_puppet_of = TUR
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				is_subject_of = TUR
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_government = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -3
				TUR = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.8.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			FROM = { 
				create_wargoal = {
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
				end_puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = { id = ottoman.10 hours = 8 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				any_other_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_guaranteed = PREV
					NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				any_other_country = {
					is_major = yes
					has_subject = PREV
					NOT = { original_tag = TUR }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

				}

	}

				has_government = FROM

				add = 25
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}

					target = FROM
					value > 30
				}

	id = ottoman.36
	title = ottoman.36.t
	desc = ottoman.36.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.36.a
		clr_country_flag = TUR_yildiz_teskilati_election
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = TUR_government_without_majority
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_government_without_majority
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			elections_allowed = no
			name = TUR_sultanate_party
			long_name = TUR_sultanate_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				date < 1914.1.10
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mehmed_said
		}
		else = {
			add_country_leader_role = {
   		        character = TUR_said_halim
    		    promote_leader = yes
    		    country_leader = {
        	    	ideology = theocracy_ideology
        	    	expire = "1965.1.1.1"
        	    	traits = { TUR_conservative_politician grand_vizier }
    		    }
		    }
		}
		TUR_remove_party_factionalism = yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
}

    }

###Elections late 1912
country_event = {
	id = ottoman.45
	title = ottoman.45.t
	desc = ottoman.45.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		date > 1912.6.1
		date < 1913.1.1
		has_country_leader = {
			character = TUR_ahmed_muhtar
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		has_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
		has_elections = yes
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		###Liberal victory
		name = ottoman.45.a
		set_country_flag = liberal_victory
		promote_character = TUR_mehmed_kamil
		add_stability = 0.1
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.3
		}
		set_politics = {
		    ruling_party = democratic
    	    election_frequency = 48
		    elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_ideas = TUR_ittihadist_plot
		TUR_remove_minority_focuses = yes
		set_country_flag = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory
		unlock_national_focus = TUR_hurriyet_ve_itilaf_victory
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_PROTECT_DEMOCRACY
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_VATAN_VE_HURRIYET_CEMIYETI
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_THREE_PASHA_GOVERNMENT
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_ENVERS_FEVER_DREAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = TUR_ai_behavior
						option = TUR_FORM_A_LEFTIST_PARLIAMENT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		###Ittihad victory
		name = ottoman.45.b
		set_country_flag = ittihad_victory
		TUR_mahmud_sevket = {
			promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		set_politics = {
		    ruling_party = neutrality
    	    election_frequency = 48
		    elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = neutrality
			name = TUR_neutrality_party
			long_name = TUR_neutrality_party_long
		}	
		set_country_flag = TUR_elections_1912
		add_ideas = TUR_idea_liberal_revenge
		unlock_national_focus = TUR_ittihat_ve_terakki_victory
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TUR_ai_behavior
					option = TUR_HURRIYET_VE_ITILAF
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

#goeben und breslau
country_event = {
	id = ottoman.53
	title = ottoman.53.t
	desc = ottoman.53.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_destroyers
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		GER = {
			has_war_with = ENG
		}
		TUR = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = GER
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.53.a
		GER = {
			transfer_ship = {
				prefer_name = "SMS Goeben"
				type = battle_cruiser
				target = TUR
			}
			transfer_ship = {
				prefer_name = "SMS Breslau"
				type = light_cruiser
				target = TUR
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_character = GER_wilhelm_souchon
				}
				GER_wilhelm_souchon = {
					set_nationality = TUR
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_goeben_und_breslau
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = ottoman.54
					hours = 8
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.53.b
		GER = {
			destroy_ships = {
				type = ship_hull_cruiser
				count = 1
			}
			destroy_ships = {
				type = ship_hull_heavy
				count = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = ottoman.55
					hours = 8
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

						is_owned_by = RUS

							is_subject_of = RUS
							not = { tag = TUR }
						}
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = TUR
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			TUR = {
				country_event = {
					id = ottoman.72
					hours = 8
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				is_in_faction_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 10
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_opinion = {

			}
		}
	}

			}

country_event = { #islamist victory in elections
	id = ottoman.118
	title = ottoman.118.t
	desc = ottoman.118.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_conservative_victory
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = TUR_pardon_conservatives
		is_power_balance_in_range = {
    		id = TUR_conservative_liberal
    		range < TUR_conservative_liberal_conservative_balanced
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = TUR_conservatives_in_charge
			has_country_flag = TUR_al_qahtaniya_empowered
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.118.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_unlock_said_i_nursi_path
		set_country_flag = TUR_said_i_nursi_path
		set_country_flag = TUR_conservatives_in_charge
		clr_country_flag = TUR_liberals_in_charge
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = democratic
			long_name = TUR_islamist_party_long
			name = TUR_islamist_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = TUR_said_i_nursi_leader
					has_country_flag = TUR_mustafa_sabri_leader
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
   		        character = TUR_said_i_nursi
    		    promote_leader = yes
    		    country_leader = {
        	    	ideology = conservatism
        	    	expire = "1965.1.1.1"
        	    	traits = { islamist_modern_leader grand_vizier }
    		    }
		    }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_said_i_nursi_leader
			}
			promote_character = TUR_said_i_nursi
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_mustafa_sabri_leader
			}
			promote_character = TUR_mustafa_sabri
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_modern_islamism_done
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_synthesis_of_the_old_and_the_new
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_increase_medrese_education_done
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_increase_medrese_education_idea
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_form_volunteers_from_conservatives_done
				has_war = no
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_conservative_volunteers1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_form_volunteers_from_conservatives_done
				has_war = yes
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_conservative_volunteers2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_increase_sect_membership_done
			}
			add_ideas = TUR_empowered_sects
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_reform_mecelle_done
			}
			add_ideas = reformed_mecelle2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_guarantee_personal_freedoms_done
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_guaranteed_human_right
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = reformed_mecelle_done
			}
			remove_ideas = reformed_mecelle
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = secular_civil_code_done
			}
			remove_ideas = secular_civil_code
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = autonomous_civil_code_done
			}
			remove_ideas = autonomous_civil_code
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = TUR_status_of_autonomy_done
			}
			remove_ideas = TUR_autonomous_vilayets
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		country_event = ottoman.164
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #population exchange between the ottomans
	id = ottoman.124
	title = ottoman.124.t
	desc = ottoman.124.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.124.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			TUR = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_state = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
							is_controlled_by = TUR
						}
					}
					random_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
							is_controlled_by = TUR
						}
						set_temp_variable = {
							TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
						}
						divide_temp_variable = {
							TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
						}
						add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
						clr_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
						set_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_1
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = GRE
							is_controlled_by = GRE
							is_core_of = GRE
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							multiply_temp_variable = {
								TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
							}
							add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
						}
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_population_to_state
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_state = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
							is_controlled_by = TUR
							NOT = {
								has_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_1
							}
						}
					}
					random_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
							is_controlled_by = TUR
						}
						set_temp_variable = {
							TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
						}
						divide_temp_variable = {
							TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
						}
						add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
						clr_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
						set_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_2
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = GRE
							is_controlled_by = GRE
							is_core_of = GRE
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							multiply_temp_variable = {
								TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
							}
							add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
						}
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_population_to_state
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_state = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
							is_controlled_by = TUR
							NOT = {
								has_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_2
							}
						}
					}
					random_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
							is_controlled_by = TUR
						}
						set_temp_variable = {
							TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
						}
						divide_temp_variable = {
							TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
						}
						add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
						clr_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = GRE
							is_controlled_by = GRE
							is_core_of = GRE
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							multiply_temp_variable = {
								TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
							}
							add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
						}
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_population_to_state
					}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_send_greeks_to_greece
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = GRE
					modifier = TUR_agreed_to_population_exchange
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottoman.125 hours = 8 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 70
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.124.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			TUR = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = GRE
					modifier = TUR_refused_to_population_exchange
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottoman.126 hours = 8 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = ottoman.125.d

	option = {
		name = ottoman.125.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
				}

				}

				}

				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
				clr_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
				set_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_1
				set_state_flag = TUR_unintended_consequence_failed_greek_infrastructure
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = GRE
					is_controlled_by = GRE
					is_core_of = GRE
				}

					multiply_temp_variable = {
						TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
					}
					add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower

			}
		}

			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_1
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
				}
				add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
				clr_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
				set_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_2
				set_state_flag = TUR_unintended_consequence_failed_greek_infrastructure
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
				    is_owned_by = GRE
				    is_controlled_by = GRE
				    is_core_of = GRE
			    }
				hidden_effect = {
					multiply_temp_variable = {
						TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
					}
					add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_population_to_state
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_2
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
				}
				add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_greek_minority }
				clr_state_flag = TUR_greek_state
				set_state_flag = TUR_unintended_consequence_failed_greek_infrastructure
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = GRE

		}

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GRE
			modifier = TUR_agreed_to_population_exchange

			ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes
		}

			base = 5
		}
	}

country_event = { #population exchange between the ottomans disagreed
	id = ottoman.126
	title = ottoman.126.t
	desc = ottoman.126.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.126.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece2
			}
			unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_deport_greeks
			set_country_flag = TUR_deport_greeks_flag
		}
		else = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = GRE
				modifier = TUR_refused_to_population_exchange
			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece_not
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
  				focus = TUR_population_exchange_with_greece
  				uncomplete_children = no
  				refund_political_power = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
}

		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_southslav_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_4
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {

						state = 756

						state = 200

					}

			}

		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = BUL
			modifier = TUR_agreed_to_population_exchange
		}

country_event = { #deport romanians agreed
	id = ottoman.137
	title = ottoman.137.t
	desc = ottoman.137.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ottoman.137.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
				}
				add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
				clr_state_flag = TUR_romanian_state
				set_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_7
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROM
					is_controlled_by = ROM
					is_core_of = ROM
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					multiply_temp_variable = {
						TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
					}
					add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_population_to_state
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_7
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
				}
				add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
				clr_state_flag = TUR_romanian_state
				set_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_8
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
				    is_owned_by = ROM
				    is_controlled_by = ROM
				    is_core_of = ROM
			    }
				hidden_effect = {
					multiply_temp_variable = {
						TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
					}
					add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_population_to_state
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_state = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_8
					}
				}
			}
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
					is_controlled_by = TUR
				}
				set_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
				}
				divide_temp_variable = {
					TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
				}
				add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_romanian_minority }
				clr_state_flag = TUR_romanian_state
			}
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ROM
					is_controlled_by = ROM
					is_core_of = ROM
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					multiply_temp_variable = {
						TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
					}
					add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_population_to_state
			}
		}
		unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_send_romanians_to_romania
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ROM
			modifier = TUR_agreed_to_population_exchange
		}
		set_country_flag = TUR_can_deport_romanians
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottoman.139 days = 18 }
			ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
}

			}
			set_country_flag = TUR_relocate_armenians_to_the_east_not
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
  				focus = TUR_relocate_armenians_to_the_east
  				uncomplete_children = no
  				refund_political_power = no
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}

							is_controlled_by = GEO
							is_core_of = GEO
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							multiply_temp_variable = {
								TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
							}
							add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
						}
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_population_to_state
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						any_owned_state = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
							is_controlled_by = TUR
							NOT = {
								has_state_flag = TUR_previous_state_12
							}
						}
					}
					random_owned_state = {
						limit = {
							has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
							is_controlled_by = TUR
						}
						set_temp_variable = {
							TUR_target_state_manpower = state_population
						}
						divide_temp_variable = {
							TUR_target_state_manpower = -5
						}
						add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
						remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_georgian_minority }
						clr_state_flag = TUR_georgian_state
						set_state_flag = TUR_unintended_consequence_georgians_to_georgia
					}
					random_state = {
						limit = {
							is_owned_by = GEO
							is_controlled_by = GEO
							is_core_of = GEO
						}
						hidden_effect = {
							multiply_temp_variable = {
								TUR_target_state_manpower = -1
							}
							add_manpower = var:TUR_target_state_manpower
						}
						custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_add_population_to_state
					}
				}
				unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_send_georgians_to_georgia
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = GEO
					modifier = TUR_agreed_to_population_exchange
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottoman.129 hours = 8 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 50
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value > 70
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.144.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			TUR = {
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = GEO
					modifier = TUR_refused_to_population_exchange
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ottoman.130 hours = 8 }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				has_war_with = FROM
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < -50
				}
			}
		}
	}

		}

			base = 5
		}
	}

country_event = { #asir rebellion
	id = ottoman.163
	title = ottoman.163.t
	desc = ottoman.163.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TUR
		any_owned_state = {
			is_core_of = ASR
		}
		date > 1910.10.1
		OR = {
			747 = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority } }
			662 = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority } }
		}
		NOT = {
			country_exists = ASR
			TUR = {
				has_government = democratic
				has_completed_focus = TUR_modern_islamism
				has_completed_focus = TUR_power_of_the_caliph
				has_completed_focus = TUR_for_the_good_of_the_arabs
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_asir_rebellion
	option = {
		name = ottoman.163.a
		set_global_flag = asir_rebellion
		if = {
			limit = {
				TUR = {
					owns_state = 747
				}
			}
			747 = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_ottoman_arab_minority_modify_resistance_target_10
				add_to_variable = {
					TUR_ottoman_resistance_target = 0.1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				TUR = {
					NOT = {
						owns_state = 747
					}
					owns_state = 662
				}
			}
			662 = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_ottoman_arab_minority_modify_resistance_target_10
				add_to_variable = {
					TUR_ottoman_resistance_target = 0.1
				}
			}
		}
		activate_mission = TUR_brewing_asir_rebellion
		unlock_decision_tooltip = TUR_truce_with_asir
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #yemen declares autonomy
	id = ottoman.167
	title = ottoman.167.t
	desc = ottoman.167.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_yemen_autonomy
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = YEM
				}
				transfer_state_to = YEM
			}
			add_state_claim = PREV
			293 = {
				clr_state_flag = TUR_autonomous_region
				remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_autonomous_region scope = TUR }
				clr_state_flag = TUR_autonomous_region_not_control
				set_state_flag = TUR_arab_state
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_controlled_by = TUR
					}
					add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = TUR_arab_minority }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_controlled_by = TUR
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = TUR_arab_state_nocontrol
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.167.a
		set_country_flag = TUR_treaty_of_daan_autonomy
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = YEM
				}
				transfer_state_to = YEM
			}
		}
		set_autonomy = {
   		    target = YEM
    		autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
    		end_wars = yes
    		end_civil_wars = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TUR_treaty_of_daan_autonomy_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			YEM = {
				add_ideas = TUR_wavering_ottoman_influence
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = TUR
				}
				white_peace = YEM
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 30
				enemies_strength_ratio < 0.3
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ottoman.167.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = YEM
				}
				transfer_state_to = YEM
			}
		}
		declare_war_on = {
            target = YEM
            type = annex_everything
        }
		hidden_effect = {
			YEM = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					neutrality = 100
				}
			}
			ottoman_minority_variable_check = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				enemies_strength_ratio > 0.3
			}
		}
	}
}

		tag = TUR

			}

    			artillery_equipment < 1

    			howitzer_equipment < 1
			}

			is_major = yes

				controls_state = 860
				controls_state = 341

			}
		}
	}

		name = ottoman.207.a

		retire_country_leader = yes
		uncomplete_national_focus = {
  			focus = TUR_undermine_democracy
  			uncomplete_children = yes

		}
		complete_national_focus = TUR_protect_democracy
		promote_character = TUR_ahmet_izzet
		hidden_effect = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
	}
}

# GOEBEN AND BRESLAU NEWS

news_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.109
	title = ww1_ottoman.109.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.109.desc
	picture = ww1_ottoman_109
	is_triggered_only = yes
	major = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = GER
				}
				transfer_ship = {
					prefer_name = "SMS Goeben"
					type = battle_cruiser
					target = TUR
				}
				transfer_ship = {
					prefer_name = "SMS Breslau"
					type = light_cruiser
					target = TUR
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character = GER_wilhelm_souchon
					}
					GER_wilhelm_souchon = {
						set_nationality = TUR
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.109.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				has_war_with = ENG
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.109.b
		trigger = {
			original_tag = TUR
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.109.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = ENG
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
				has_war_with = GER
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.109.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				original_tag = ENG
				is_in_faction_with = ENG
				has_war_with = GER
				original_tag = GER
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				has_war_with = ENG
				original_tag = TUR
			}
		}
	}
}

		}

country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.112
	title = ww1_ottoman.112.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.112.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.112.a
		set_global_flag = caucasus_collapsed
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = PER
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = GEO
					is_core_of = PER
					NOT = {
						state = 229
						state = 823
						state = 818
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = PER
			}
			else = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_owned_by = GEO
						is_core_of = PER
						NOT = {
							is_core_of = AZR
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = PER
				}
			}
		}
		AZR = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = GEO
					is_core_of = AZR
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = TUR
					}
				}
				transfer_state_to = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AZR = {
					OR = {
						is_subject = no
						is_subject_of = RUS
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_subject_autonomy_feature = yes
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = AZR
					autonomous_state = autonomy_tgwr_informal_protectorate
					freedom_level = 0.6
				}
				AZR = {
					set_country_flag = protectorate
				}
				else = {
					puppet = AZR
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				AZR = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic
					}
					set_popularities = {
						fascism = 28
						communism = 18
						democratic = 46
						neutrality = 8
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = GEO
				OR = {
					is_core_of = TUR
					is_core_of = ARM
					is_claimed_by = TUR
					state = 748
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 230
				}
			}
			TUR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GEO = {
					owns_state = 230
				}
			}
			ARM = {
				transfer_state = 230
			}
		}
		GEO = {
			drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				set_state_owner = 231
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_core_of = ARM
							is_core_of = AZR
						}
						NOT = {
							state = 816
							state = 748
							state = 231
							state = 233
						}
					}
					GEO = {
						remove_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = neutrality
					long_name = GEO_neutrality_party
					name = GEO_neutrality_party
				}
				set_research_slots = 2
				set_stability = 0.56
				GEO_noe_zhordania = {
					promote_character = authoritarian_democracy
					promote_character = socialism
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				GER = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			GER = {
				country_event = ww1_ottoman.113
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					FRA = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				FRA = {
					country_event = ww1_ottoman.113
				}
			}
		}
		news_event = ww1_ottoman.132
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					MOU = {
						exists = no
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					release = MOU
				}
				MOU = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = democratic
					}
				}
			}
			# Baku Commune
			if = {
				limit = {
					AZR = {
						exists = yes
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
						any_owned_state = {
							is_core_of = PREV
							NOT = { state = 229 }
						}
					}
				}
				AZR = {
					start_civil_war = {
						ideology = communism
						size = 0.2
						capital = 64
						states = { 229 }
						keep_unit_leaders_trigger = {
							OR = {
								has_trait = trait_royal
								has_trait = trait_royalist
								has_trait = old_guard
								has_trait = politically_connected
								has_trait = old_guard_navy
							}
						}
						keep_all_characters = yes
						PREV = {
							AZR_stepan_shaumianv = {
								set_nationality = PREV.PREV
							}
						}
						promote_character = AZR_stepan_shaumianv
						add_country_leader_trait = standing_alone
						set_party_name = {
							ideology = communism
							long_name = BAK_communism_party
							name = BAK_communism_party
						}
						set_party_name = {
							ideology = fascism
							long_name = BAK_fascism_party
							name = BAK_fascism_party
						}
						set_cosmetic_tag = AZR_BAK_communism
					}
					set_state_controller = 229
					BAK = { set_province_controller = 7661 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

			target = GEO
			modifier = small_decrease
		}

			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

					is_neighbor_of = GEO

					is_neighbor_of = GEO

			set_party_name = {
				ideology = neutrality
				long_name = TUR_neutrality_party_long
				name = TUR_neutrality_party
			}
		}

		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}

					target = FROM

# International Suez
country_event = {
	id = ww1_ottoman.134
	title = ww1_ottoman.134.t
	desc = ww1_ottoman.134.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tur_politician_march
	trigger = {
		tag = TUR
		has_war = no
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = frankfurt_treaty
			has_global_flag = versallies_treaty
		}
		owns_state = 454
		owns_state = 856
		has_country_flag = great_war_winner
		has_country_flag = ottomans_lost_jerusalem
		447 = {
			OR = {
				is_owned_by = PREV
				EGY = {
					is_subject = no
					owns_state = PREV
				}
				any_other_country = {
					has_country_flag = great_war_loser
					owns_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ottomans_hold_cairo_and_alexandria
			has_subject = EGY
			country_exists = PAL
			country_exists = ISR
			owns_state = 446
			has_border_war_with = EGY
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 140
	}
	option = {
		name = ww1_ottoman.134.a
		hidden_effect = {
			PAL = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = PAL_international
				add_ideas = PAL_moj
				add_ideas = PAL_sectarian_divide
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = great_war_loser
						AND = {
							original_tag = EGY
							is_subject = no
						}
						is_subject_of = PREV
					}
					OR = {
						owns_state = 447
						owns_state = 453
						owns_state = 454
						owns_state = 856
						owns_state = 858
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = ww1_ottoman.135
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 447
					state = 453
					state = 454
					state = 856
					state = 858
				}
			}
			add_core_of = PAL
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = PREV
				}
				transfer_state_to = PAL
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_subject_autonomy_feature = yes
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PAL
				autonomy_state = autonomy_tgwr_protectorate
			}
			PAL = { set_country_flag = protectorate }
			else = {
				puppet = PAL
				PAL = { add_ideas = protectorate }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_major = yes
					NOT = {
						has_war_with = PAL
						has_war_with = TUR
						has_war_with = GER
						has_war_with = FRA
					}
				}
				set_truce = {
					target = PAL
					days = 365
				}
				PAL = {
					give_military_access = PREV
				}
			}
			PAL = {
				set_capital = { state = 454 }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_popularities = {
					democratic = 34
					neutrality = 65
				}
				country_lock_all_division_template = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
